- **Session wrap-up / handoff note**: this whole session (2026-07-18/19) traces back to the account owner relaying third-party feedback that the codebase "isn't written professionally" and asking what a real engineer would change given time. Answer given up front: TypeScript, a bundler, and a lightweight reactive framework would each be real improvements — confirmed via `AskUserQuestion` to start with the lowest-risk one first and keep deploying normally throughout, then given standing authorization ("продовжуй завжди без питань") to keep executing through the rest without re-confirming each routine step. Shipped, in order:
  1. **Vite bundler, 4 phases**: Phase 1 (build tooling only, deploy-inert) → Phase 2 (wired Firebase Hosting to the real `dist/` build, `predeploy` hook, `scripts/build-site.mjs` auto-generating `sw.js`'s precache list) → Phase 3 (`dist-smoke` CI job so the bundled artifact gets the same automated coverage source already had) → Phase 4 (`window.__RYTM_TEST_HOOKS__`, closing the last test-compatibility gap so `dist-smoke` could run the *full* 20-test suite instead of a 3-test subset). GitHub Pages deliberately still serves unbundled source — no tool available here can flip its Settings → Pages build-source toggle.
  2. **TypeScript, 3 phases**: gradual, JSDoc-based, zero file renames, zero runtime changes — `js/tx-validation.js` → `functions/lib/pure.js` (needed its own `functions/tsconfig.json`, CJS vs the root project's ESM) → `functions/lib/monobank.js`. Both `functions/lib/sweep.js` (Firestore-snapshot typing, a real design decision) and any `js/*.js` file touching `AppState` are explicitly flagged in `CLAUDE.md` as bigger steps, not casual next picks.
  3. **Preact, proof of concept**: one widget (`js/debt.js`'s payoff-forecast chart), vendored (not npm-installed) for the same GitHub-Pages-unbundled reason as Tesseract. A real bug was caught and fixed during verification (a vendored-but-fully-inlined file left stale in `dist/`'s precache list, which would have 404'd the service worker's `cache.addAll()` in production) — worth remembering as a general pattern for *any* future vendored dependency that ends up statically (not dynamically) imported.
  - **Explicit next-session candidates, in rough order of how contained they are**: (a) opt `functions/lib/sweep.js` into TypeScript — needs a real decision on how deeply to type Firestore snapshot/doc shapes first; (b) whether/how to expand Preact beyond the one proof-of-concept widget — an open conversation, not a decided direction; (c) the still-standing GitHub Pages build-pipeline divergence (Pages serves source, Hosting serves the Vite bundle) — blocked on a manual repo Settings toggle only the account owner can do.
  - Every PR this session (#246–#253) went through the same loop: branch → PR → CI → squash-merge → (deploy, when the change actually reached what's served) → log here — no exceptions, including two PRs (#252, #253) correctly identified as not needing a Hosting redeploy since `functions/` isn't part of the Vite-bundled `js/` graph.
- **TypeScript adoption — Phase 4 (`functions/lib/sweep.js`), picking up the next-session candidate (a) from the handoff note above ("продовжуй")** (PR [#254](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/254), squash-merged as `527bb18` after all three CI jobs — `smoke`, `dist-smoke`, `firestore-rules` — went green with no review comments): opted the last, most-coupled `lib/` file into `// @ts-check`. Resolved the Firestore-snapshot-typing question CLAUDE.md flagged as the real design decision here by **not** importing firebase-admin's real types at all — this repo's CI never runs `npm install` inside `functions/` before `npm run typecheck`, so those types aren't reliably resolvable there — and instead describing `db`/`sendPushFn`/every Firestore snapshot with small structural typedefs covering only the members this file actually reads (`.exists`, `.data()`, `.id`, `.docs`, `.empty`, `.ref.delete()`/`.set()`), matching the shape the fakes in `tests/functions-sweep.mjs` already implement; `db` itself stays `any` (faithfully typing Firestore's real chained builder API wasn't worth it for a function that only ever calls `.doc(path).get()`/`.collection(path).get()`). One line rewritten to satisfy the checker, confirmed behaviorally identical: `walletCurrency`'s `(wallets.find(...) || {}).currency` → `wallets.find(...)?.currency` (both produce `undefined` on a miss). `npm run typecheck` was clean on the first pass — no real type errors surfaced, `strict:false` project-wide meant the null-safety edge cases that would otherwise need touching (e.g. `r.amount` narrowing after an `if(!r.amount) continue`) never actually flagged.
  - **Deploy decision, made from an actual diff, not a vibe call** (per CLAUDE.md's explicit caution in the Commands section, added after the Zminka/Rytm stale-deploy incident): `git diff b9821d6 origin/main -- functions/` — `b9821d6` (Monobank integration) is the last commit whose `functions/` changes were actually redeployed (confirmed via its own CHANGELOG entry: "Deployed all relevant targets: `firebase deploy --only functions,hosting`"). Everything since then (`4328c3f`/`3bbb8e7`/this PR's `06f3244`) is `// @ts-check` pragmas, JSDoc typedefs, and comments only, plus this PR's one behaviorally-identical `walletCurrency` rewrite — confirmed by reading the actual diff hunks, not inferring from the commit messages. **No Cloud Functions redeploy needed or performed.** No `firestore.rules`/Hosting-visible changes either (`functions/tsconfig.json` is a new file but build/check-time only, never loaded at runtime by the deployed function) — nothing to redeploy on any target this time.

- **Preact adoption — 3rd widget, the FX rates widget, closing out candidate (b)'s authorized "1-2 more widgets" batch** (PR [#258](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/258), squash-merged as `b7e799e` after all three CI jobs went green with no review comments — see the flakiness fix below for why the first CI run failed): converted `js/settings-managers.js`'s `renderFxWidget()` → `#fx-widget-list` (the Finance tab's currency-rate row list) — same profile as the prior two widgets: pure, read-only, computed entirely from `AppState.currencyRates`, single call site, previously rebuilt in full via `innerHTML=` on every render. New small stateless `FxWidgetRow` component, keyed by currency code. The sibling `renderRatesList()` (the editable Rates manager modal, with a live number input per row) deliberately left as manual `innerHTML=` — real edit interactions, a bigger conversion than this initiative's conservative pace intends.
  - New `tests/fx-widget-rates.mjs` (no prior test covered this widget): default seed rates render as 4 real rows, and editing a rate via the Rates manager (opened by clicking the widget itself) updates the corresponding row in place with no duplicate/stale row left behind. Wired into both `smoke-test.yml` jobs.
  - **Real CI failure, found and fixed within the same PR** (pushed directly to the PR's own branch, per this file's standing convention for Codex-PR fixes extended here to a self-authored PR's own CI failure): the first CI run failed both `smoke` and `dist-smoke` with `expected USD's seed rate (41) in the widget, got {"rate":"44,67 грн"}`. Root cause: `js/app-init.js`'s `init()` unconditionally calls `maybeAutoUpdateRates()` on cold start, which fetches live NBU rates in the background — this sandbox's own network blocks `bank.gov.ua` (see CLAUDE.md's "expected sandbox noise" note elsewhere in this file), which is exactly why the test looked deterministic when verified locally before opening the PR, but a GitHub Actions runner has real internet access, so the live fetch actually succeeded there and silently replaced the seed rate before the assertion ran. Fixed by blocking `bank.gov.ua`/`allorigins.win`/the `privat-rates` proxy via `page.route()` in the test itself, matching how every other network dependency in this test suite is stubbed rather than left to the environment's actual reachability. Second CI run (after the fix, `6ad4f7f`) went green on all three jobs.

No `functions/`/`firestore.rules` changes in this PR (confirmed via the diff, not assumed). GitHub Pages mirror auto-deploys on push to `main`. Wired into both CI jobs.
  - **Real bug found by Codex's automated PR review, fixed in the same PR before merge** (pushed directly to the PR's own branch, per this file's standing convention): `toggleWidget()` only called `applyWidgetVisibility()`, which renders from whatever's already cached — if a user had `cryptoTop` disabled at cold init (the only production `maybeRefreshCryptoTop()` call site, which returns immediately when the widget starts disabled), re-enabling it later via the Widgets manager never triggered a fetch, leaving the section hidden indefinitely until a full page reload. Fixed by also calling `maybeRefreshCryptoTop()` from `toggleWidget()` (safe unconditionally — it already no-ops when the widget is off or the cache is still fresh). Added a matching regression case to `tests/dashboard-widgets.mjs` (disable with cache cleared → confirm hidden → re-enable → confirm a fresh fetch happens and the section reappears). Investigated live via `recaptchaenterprise.googleapis.com`/`identitytoolkit.googleapis.com` REST calls (same service-account credentials used for the App Check provisioning work): the mismatched key is real and legitimate — Firebase's own auto-provisioned "Key for Identity Platform reCAPTCHA integration" (created 2026-07-08), registered correctly in Identity Platform's `recaptchaConfig.recaptchaKeys`, `allowAllDomains: true` (not a domain-restriction issue), backing the **reCAPTCHA SMS Defense** feature SETUP.md already recommends (`phoneEnforcementState: "AUDIT"`, confirmed live — the feature is genuinely active, not a stale doc). **Working hypothesis, not yet confirmed**: two different reCAPTCHA Enterprise site keys loading on the same page (the manually-created App Check key + Firebase's own auto-injected SMS Defense key) may be conflicting with each other under the shared global `grecaptcha.enterprise` namespace — a follow-up live screenshot showed App Check itself then getting a `403` from `content-firebaseappcheck.googleapis.com` and entering the SDK's own 24-hour client-side throttle (`appCheck/initial-throttle`), even though the App Check key's own server-side config (site key, provider registration) checked out correctly via the same REST calls. This may be the actual root cause of the App Check verified-rate crash investigated earlier in this file (superseding the earlier TWA-correlation hypothesis, which remains unconfirmed either way).

- **App-wide +1px font-scale shift, prompted by direct subjective account-owner feedback** ("шрифт замалий" — comparing this chat interface's own body text against the app's): the earlier "12px floor" passes in this file only ever bumped the smallest outliers, never the app's actual everyday-reading baseline (most row names/labels/values sat one step above the floor, at 12-13px). Shifted the whole small-text scale up by exactly 1px across the board — `12px→13px`, `12.5px→13.5px`, `13px→14px`, `13.5px→14.5px`, `14px→15px` — roughly 150 `font-size` declarations across `index.html` and 6 `js/*.js` files with inline template styles, via a two-pass `sed` through unique placeholder tokens so the 5 buckets couldn't cascade into each other. `15px`+ left untouched (already comfortably sized). See CLAUDE.md's new "App-wide +1px font-scale shift" bullet (Mobile UI redesign section) for the full detail — logged here per the standing session convention, promoted there since it's a durable baseline future font work needs to know about.

First pass caught one hit (`.fin-mini-stat-label`) that was a false positive of the *detection script itself* — that element already used `white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis` before this change too, and an ellipsis element's `scrollWidth` always exceeds its `clientWidth` by design (that's the mechanism behind the "…", not breakage). Excluded that exact CSS-property combination from the check and got a clean pass with zero real overflow findings.

  - **15th (`js/analytics-csv.js`, PR [#280](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/280))** — the first of the Preact-using files and the one that resolved the recurring `h()`-typing friction that had been blocking every Preact file: TypeScript was inferring `h`'s signature from the *vendored* `js/vendor/preact/preact.module.js`'s own minified runtime (3 declared params, extra children read via `arguments.length`) rather than the real `preact` npm package's richer `.d.ts`, because a real resolvable local `.js` file wins over an ambient wildcard module declaration for the same specifier. Fixed once, systemically: installed `preact` as a type-only devDependency (never imported by bare specifier in real runtime source — Preact stays vendored locally, this is purely for `tsc` to have real types to source), added `types/preact-vendor.d.ts` (ambient wildcard `declare module '*vendor/preact/preact.module.js' { export * from 'preact'; }`), and a per-file pattern reused identically across every subsequent Preact file: `import { h as _h, render, Fragment } from './vendor/preact/preact.module.js'; /** @type {typeof import('preact').h} */ const h = /** @type {any} */ (_h);` — a real local re-declaration with an explicit type annotation wins inference where the ambient declaration alone didn't. Also fixed a real CI flakiness bug in the same PR (pushed directly to its branch, per this file's standing convention): `tests/e2e-crud.mjs` timed out on `page.goto(...,{waitUntil:'networkidle'})` on a real GitHub Actions runner — same root cause as `tests/smoke.mjs`/`tests/fx-widget-rates.mjs`'s earlier flakiness this session (this sandbox blocks `bank.gov.ua`/`allorigins.win`/`api.coingecko.com` outright and fails fast; a real runner has internet access and a slow/hanging live fetch instead) — fixed with the same three `page.route(...).abort()` blocks already used elsewhere. `CACHE_NAME` `v87`→`v88`, deployed.
  - **16th (`js/dashboard-widgets.js`, PR [#281](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/281))**: only needed the `h`-cast pattern above, smallest Preact file. `CACHE_NAME` `v88`→`v89`, deployed.
  - **17th (`js/debt.js`, PR [#282](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/282))**: `h`-cast pattern for `DebtBurndownChart`/`DebtForecastText`, plus the usual DOM casts and a couple of genuinely-identical-output rewrites (`isNaN(d)`→`isNaN(d.getTime())`, Date arithmetic → `.getTime()`, `.replace('{n}',n)`→`.replace('{n}',String(n))`, `h('br')`→`h('br',null)` since Preact's real typed overloads require ≥2 args even though the runtime tolerates fewer) and a `DebtForecastText` props typedef marking `n`/`avgStr` optional (the done/no-pace states never pass them). `CACHE_NAME` `v89`→`v90`, deployed.
  - **18th (`js/color-picker.js`, PR [#283](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/283))**: only one cast needed all file. **Real bug caught in my own added JSDoc, not the original code**: `seedConfigFromDocs()` was first annotated `@returns {void}` without checking call sites; `tsc` immediately flagged two callers testing the return value's truthiness, and the function actually does return a real boolean — corrected the annotation to `@returns {boolean}`. Comment/cast-only otherwise, bundle unchanged, no deploy.
  - **19th (`js/settings-managers.js`, PR [#284](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/284))**, largest file at 1104 lines: `h`-cast pattern for `FxWidgetRow`; a custom DOM expando (`overlay._returnFocusTo`, used by `setupModalAccessibility()`'s focus-restore) typed via an intersection type (`HTMLElement & {_returnFocusTo?: HTMLElement | null}`); `window.ICON_NAMES` added to `types/globals.d.ts`'s `Window` augmentation; ~20 DOM casts across the wallets/categories/budgets/rates/FX-converter/widgets managers. `CACHE_NAME` `v90`→`v91`, deployed. This closed out all 4 Preact-rendered widgets (debt payoff-forecast, analytics donut, FX rates, and this file's own FX-widget-row usage) under `@ts-check`.
  - **20th (`js/core.js`, PR [#285](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/285))**: new friction class — the file's 5 pinned gstatic CDN Firebase imports (`firebase-app.js`/`-app-check.js`/`-firestore.js`/`-auth.js`/`-messaging.js`) had no local file for `tsc` to resolve at all (`TS2307`), unlike the vendored-Preact case above (no real file competing for resolution this time). Fixed with `types/firebase-vendor.d.ts`, an ambient module mapping each exact pinned URL to the real `firebase` npm package's own types (installed as a type-only devDependency, pinned to the same `12.11.0` SDK version already in use). Remaining errors were familiar DOM-cast patterns (`.style`, `.options`, `.closest`), a `[RegExp,string][]` tuple TS had widened to `(RegExp|string)[][]`, and `window.__applyLangDynamic` (added to `types/globals.d.ts`). **Ripple effect into an already-checked file, caught by the whole-project `npm run typecheck` run this sweep has done after every foundational-file PR**: `js/firebase-sync.js`'s `loadProfilesMeta()` assigns `snap.data()` straight into `AppState.profilesMeta` — previously silent because `core.js`'s unresolved imports meant `getDoc`/`snap.data()` were untyped; now caught for real once the ambient mapping gave `DocumentData` a real shape. Fixed with one cast at the assignment site. Comment/cast-only, bundle unchanged (`app-BYEii9FT.js` byte-identical to `main`'s prior build) — deployed anyway as a defensive sync-check (this sandbox's egress proxy blocks direct requests to the live Hosting/Pages content domains, so the actually-live `CACHE_NAME` couldn't be read back to confirm files 10/11/14/15/16/17/19's deploys had all really landed; redeploying the current `dist/` is idempotent and safe, and confirmed hosting is now definitely in sync with `main`@`8cd294c`).
  - **Net progress this span**: 20 of the `js/*.js` module graph's ~24 files now opt into `// @ts-check`. Remaining: `js/app-init.js`, `js/app.js`, `js/state.js` (next up, in that order), plus `js/vendor/tesseract`/`js/vendor/preact` (never meant to be typed) and the 4 classic non-module scripts (optional, lower-priority).
- **Icon polish, prompted by the account owner sharing 4 screenshots and asking to replace some small icons plus fix "arrows poking out of a green background"** (PR [#289](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/289), squash-merged as `9cdb2dc` after CI went green with no review comments — Codex's automated review commented only that it had hit its own usage limit, not an actual finding): the vague "профілю" ("profile") framing in the request turned out to mean the "Наближається платіж"/"Повторювані операції" settings rows (`ic-notif-recurring`/`ic-set-recurring`, green `#10b981` badges) rather than the avatar picker (`BUILTIN_AVATARS`) — confirmed by actually reproducing the exact screenshots locally (a stubbed-Firebase Playwright pass through Settings/Analytics/the avatar picker) rather than guessing from the text description alone, since "which icon" was resolvable from the code/screenshots and didn't need an `AskUserQuestion` round-trip.
  - **Root cause, confirmed by pixel-measuring a zoomed render, not just eyeballing it**: the `repeat`/`swap` glyphs' own coordinates in `js/classic-globals.js`'s `ICON_PATHS` sat only ~2-3 units from their 24×24 viewBox edge. Mathematically the icon's own bounding box was still always safely inscribed inside its circular badge (a 17px `.ico` inside a 34px `.icon-badge` circle has ~5px of slack even in the worst-case corner-to-corner diagonal) — there was never a real clipping bug — but the diagonal arrowhead strokes reaching toward the corners read visually as "poking out." Redrew both glyphs with roughly double the vertical margin, same recognizable shape/recognizability, verified via a small throwaway Playwright harness rendering every candidate icon at both real app size and zoomed-in before/after (not committed — a temporary `tmp_icon_harness.html` used locally only).
  - **`car`** (Transport category icon): added a beltline path separating the windshield from the body and switched the wheel dots from stroked to filled circles — reads more clearly as a car at 17px instead of a plain rounded-trapezoid blob.
  - **Analytics "Різниця" (net) stat card**: was reusing the shared `coin` glyph (a currency squiggle that draws its own inner circle), which doubled up visually with the stat-icon's own circular badge — a "circle-in-a-circle" look. Added a new dedicated `plusMinus` (±) icon just for this one stat card; left `coin` itself untouched everywhere else it's used (Борг/Кредит/Здоров'я/Аптека categories, crypto-top/debt-balance widgets) since those weren't the reported complaint and changing a shared glyph broadly wasn't asked for.
  - **De-duplicated `js/calendar.js`'s finance-chart best/worst-month chips**, which had raw inlined copies of the `refresh`/`swap` SVG paths (not routed through `window.Icon()` like everywhere else) — switched both to real `window.Icon()` calls so they inherit the margin fix automatically and can't drift from the shared definitions again.

No `functions/`/`firestore.rules` changes (confirmed via diff). GitHub Pages mirror auto-deploys via its own Actions workflow on push to `main` (see the candidate-c entry above — the source/dist divergence was already closed out, so no separate action needed there).   - New **`flame`** icon for the "Топ криптовалюти" widget, new **`handCoin`** icon (coin + arrow) for Борг/Кредит-repayment categories + the Debt tab's empty-state illustration + the debt-balance badge, new **`pharmacy`** (capsule, drawn as a rotated stadium-shape `<rect>` + dividing line via an inline `<g transform="rotate(45 12 12)">` — simpler and more reliable than hand-computing rotated arc coordinates) for Аптека, new **`heartPulse`** for Здоров'я — all four previously shared the generic `coin` glyph. `coin` itself is untouched and still a pickable category icon for anything else.

  - **`repeat` redrawn again**, this time reusing `refresh`'s known-good circular arc geometry (`M4 12a8 8 0 0 1 13.7-5.7L20 8` etc.) with chevron arrowheads instead of `refresh`'s L-bracket ones — differentiates the two conceptually-distinct icons (manual reload vs. recurring/looping) while both read as genuinely circular now, closing out the "кругові стрілки" (circular arrows) ask that PR #289's rectangular-loop redesign didn't fully address.
  - **Design process**: every candidate glyph (including two rejected `handCoin` attempts — a "cupped palm" and a "mitten with finger ticks," both unrecognizable as a hand at 17px, see below) was drafted and rendered via a throwaway local Playwright harness (`tmp_icon_harness.html`, never committed) at both a large size and the real 17px-icon/34px-badge production size before being wired into `ICON_PATHS` — the same verify-before-wiring approach PR #289 established. `handCoin` ended up as a coin with a single diagonal arrow through it (money passing along) rather than a literal drawn hand, since an actual hand silhouette doesn't hold up at icon size with this app's line-art style.
  - Rewired call sites: `js/core.js`'s `CAT_ICON` map (Борг/Повернення боргу/Здоров'я/Аптека) and `CAT_ICON_KEYWORDS`' `/борг/i` regex rule, `js/debt.js`'s empty-state `icon:`, `js/settings-managers.js`'s `WIDGET_DEFS` `cryptoTop` entry, `js/classic-globals.js`'s `ic-debt-balance`/`ic-crypto-top` `setIcon()` calls, and `js/analytics-csv.js`'s net-stat `window.Icon()` call. Added the 4 new thematically-category-like icons (`flame`/`handCoin`/`pharmacy`/`heartPulse`) to `window.ICON_NAMES` (the user-facing "pick a category icon" grid) per that array's own stated convention; `diffArrows` and the redrawn `repeat` are UI-conceptual, not added (matching `refresh`'s own exclusion).

- **`repeat` icon, one more round: swapped its arrowheads for `refresh`'s exact L-bracket style** (PR [#293](https://github.com/sudak666/Maxtr/pull/293), squash-merged as `aea2b79`), closing out the "arrows barely visible" complaint that PR #291's chevron redesign didn't fully fix. Sequence worth recording since it shows the right way to close out a subjective visual complaint: account owner sent a screenshot of the live "Наближається платіж" row calling the chevron tips illegible; two rounds of alternative chevron shapes (bigger legs, repositioned to the arc's true endpoint) were rendered via the same throwaway Playwright harness and still didn't read as clearly distinct arrows at 34px, confirmed with a direct side-by-side comparison screenshot sent back — at that point the account owner pointed at the existing "Скинути всі дані" row's `refresh` icon ("ось у тебе вже є майже така іконка") as the actual target: same circular-arc geometry, but its arrowhead is two perpendicular strokes (an L-bracket) rather than a narrow-angle chevron, which reads far bolder at small size without needing a filled/solid shape (an intermediate filled-triangle option was explicitly rejected — "не заливай", i.e. no fill, keep it a stroked outline like the rest of the icon set).
  - Fix: `repeat`'s arrowhead paths replaced with `refresh`'s exact `M20 4v4h-4`/`M4 20v-4h4`, making the two icons geometrically identical (arcs + arrowheads) — deliberately accepted rather than trying to invent a distinct-but-equally-legible alternative, since the two concepts (manual reload vs. recurring/looping) are already disambiguated by their different contexts/colors, not by shape alone.
  - **Held as a draft PR pending explicit visual sign-off before merging** — sent a real screenshot of the "Повторювані операції" settings row with the new arrowhead first, waited for an explicit "ок" reply, and only then marked ready-for-review and merged. Worth calling out as the right sequencing for any further subjective-taste icon tweaks this account owner asks for: render → screenshot → confirm → merge, not merge-then-ask.
  - **A local stop-hook fired mid-wait** ("uncommitted changes in the repository") while the draft PR was intentionally sitting unmerged awaiting sign-off — resolved by committing/pushing the change to its own PR branch (satisfying the hook) while explicitly leaving the PR itself in draft state, rather than merging prematurely just to quiet the hook.
